package com.instagram.clone.service;

import com.instagram.clone.dto.UserRegisterRequest;
import com.instagram.clone.dto.UserRegisterResponse;
import com.instagram.clone.entity.User;
import com.instagram.clone.repository.CommentRepository;
import com.instagram.clone.repository.PostRepository;
import com.instagram.clone.repository.UserRepository;
import jakarta.transaction.Transactional;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.boot.webmvc.autoconfigure.WebMvcProperties;
import org.springframework.security.crypto.password.PasswordEncoder;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import org.springframework.web.multipart.MultipartFile;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;

@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class UserService {

    private final UserRepository userRepository;
    private final PasswordEncoder passwordEncoder;
    private final CommentRepository commentRepository;
    private final PostRepository postRepository;
    private final CloudinaryService cloudinaryService;

    public User register(UserRegisterRequest request) {

        userRepository.findByEmail(request.getEmail())
                .ifPresent(user -> {
                    throw new RuntimeException("Email already exists");
                });

        userRepository.findByUsername(request.getUsername())
                .ifPresent(user -> {
                    throw new RuntimeException("Username already exists");
                });

        User user = User.builder()
                .username(request.getUsername())
                .email(request.getEmail())
                .password(passwordEncoder.encode(request.getPassword()))
                .bio("")
                .isPrivate(false)
                .build();

        return userRepository.save(user);
    }

    @Transactional
    public void deleteUser(Long id) {
        User user = userRepository.findById(id).orElseThrow(()-> new RuntimeException("user not found"));
        userRepository.delete(user);
    }

    public UserRegisterResponse updateBio(Long userId, String bio, String websiteUrl) {

        User user = userRepository.findById(userId)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new RuntimeException("User not found"));

        user.setBio(bio);

        if (websiteUrl != null && !websiteUrl.isBlank()) {
            String trimmed = websiteUrl.trim();
            // Auto-prepend https:// if missing scheme
            if (!trimmed.startsWith("http://") && !trimmed.startsWith("https://")) {
                trimmed = "https://" + trimmed;
            }
            // Validate it is a real URL
            try {
                new java.net.URL(trimmed).toURI();
            } catch (Exception e) {
                throw new RuntimeException("Invalid URL: please enter a valid website link.");
            }
            user.setWebsiteUrl(trimmed);
        } else {
            user.setWebsiteUrl(null);
        }

        User savedUser = userRepository.save(user);
        return mapToResponse(savedUser);
    }

    public List<UserRegisterResponse> getAllUsers() {
        return userRepository.findAll()
                .stream()
                .map(this::mapToResponse)
                .toList();
    }

    private UserRegisterResponse mapToResponse(User user) {
        return UserRegisterResponse.builder()
                .id(user.getId())
                .username(user.getUsername())
                .email(user.getEmail())
                .bio(user.getBio())
                .isPrivate(user.isPrivate())
                .createdAt(user.getCreatedAt())
                .build();
    }
    public User getUserById(Long id) {
        return userRepository.findById(id)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new RuntimeException("User not found"));
    }

    public User getUserByUsername(String username) {
        return userRepository.findByUsername(username)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new RuntimeException("User not found"));
    }

    @Transactional
    public void uploadProfilePicture(Long userId, MultipartFile file) {

        User user = userRepository.findById(userId)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new RuntimeException("User not found"));
        String contentType = file.getContentType();

        List<String> allowedTypes = Arrays.asList("image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/gif", "image/webp");

        if (contentType == null || !allowedTypes.contains(contentType)) {
            throw new RuntimeException("Only image files are allowed (JPEG, PNG, GIF, WebP)");
        }

        long maxSizeBytes = 5 * 1024 * 1024;

        if (file.getSize() > maxSizeBytes) {
            throw new RuntimeException("Profile picture must be smaller than 5 MB");
        }

        if (file.isEmpty()) {
            throw new RuntimeException("Please select a valid image file");
        }
        if (user.getProfilePicPublicId() != null) {
            cloudinaryService.deleteFile(user.getProfilePicPublicId());
        }
        Map<String, Object> uploadResult = cloudinaryService.uploadProfilePicture(file);
        String newUrl = uploadResult.get("secure_url").toString();
        String newPublicId = uploadResult.get("public_id").toString();
        user.setProfilePicUrl(newUrl);
        user.setProfilePicPublicId(newPublicId);
        userRepository.save(user);
    }


}

============================================================

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html xmlns:th="http://www.thymeleaf.org" lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8"/>
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"/>
    <title>Instagram · New Post</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" th:href="@{/css/create.css}"/>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Grand+Hotel&family=DM+Sans:wght@300;400;500;600&display=swap" rel="stylesheet"/>
</head>
<body>
<nav>
    <a class="nav-logo" th:href="@{/posts}">Instagram</a>
    <div style="font-size:16px; font-weight:600;">New post</div>
    <a class="nav-back" th:href="@{/posts}">✕</a>
</nav>

<div class="page">
    <div th:if="${error}" class="alert" style="color: red; padding: 10px; text-align: center;" th:text="${error}"></div>

    <form th:action="@{/posts/create}" method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data" id="postForm">

        <div class="modal">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <span style="color:var(--muted); font-size:14px;"></span>
                <span class="modal-title">New post</span>
                <button type="submit" class="share-btn">Share</button>
            </div>

            <div class="upload-area" id="uploadArea" onclick="document.getElementById('fileInput').click()">
                <div class="upload-icon">🏞️</div>
                <div class="upload-title">Drag photos and videos here</div>
                <div class="upload-subtitle">Share up to 10 moments with your followers</div>
                <button type="button" class="upload-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); document.getElementById('fileInput').click()">
                    Select from computer
                </button>
                <input type="file" id="fileInput" name="files" accept="image/*,video/*" multiple
                       onchange="handleFiles(this)" style="display: none;"/>
            </div>

            <div id="previewCarousel" class="preview-carousel" style="display: none;"></div>
            <div id="addMoreContainer" style="display:none; text-align:center; margin-top:10px;">
                <button type="button"
                        onclick="document.getElementById('fileInput').click()"
                        class="upload-btn">
                    + Add more
                </button>
            </div>
            <div class="details-section">
                <div class="user-row">
                    <div class="user-avatar">
                        <div class="user-avatar-inner">👤</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="user-name" th:text="${#authentication != null ? #authentication.name : 'username'}">username</div>
                </div>
                <textarea class="caption-input" name="caption"
                          placeholder="Write a caption…" maxlength="2200"
                          oninput="updateCount(this)"></textarea>
                <div class="caption-footer">
                    <span class="char-count" id="charCount">0 / 2200</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </form>
</div>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        document.querySelector('.share-btn').disabled = true;
    });
    let selectedFiles = [];

    function handleFiles(input) {
        const newFiles = Array.from(input.files);
        const maxFiles = 10;

        if (selectedFiles.length + newFiles.length > maxFiles) {
            alert('Max 10 files allowed');
            return;
        }

        selectedFiles = [...selectedFiles, ...newFiles];

        // FIX 1: Clear the input value BEFORE repopulating it
        input.value = '';

        renderPreview();
    }

    function renderPreview() {
        const area = document.getElementById('uploadArea');
        const carousel = document.getElementById('previewCarousel');
        const addMore = document.getElementById('addMoreContainer');

        if (selectedFiles.length === 0) {
            area.style.display = 'flex';
            carousel.style.display = 'none';
            addMore.style.display = 'none';
            document.querySelector('.share-btn').disabled = true;
            return;
        }

        area.style.display = 'none';
        carousel.style.display = 'flex';
        addMore.style.display = 'block';

        const shareBtn = document.querySelector('.share-btn');
        shareBtn.disabled = selectedFiles.length === 0;

        carousel.querySelectorAll('.slide-container').forEach(el => {
            const media = el.querySelector('img, video');
            if (media && media.src) {
                URL.revokeObjectURL(media.src);
            }
        });
        carousel.innerHTML = '';

        selectedFiles.forEach((file, index) => {
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);

            const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
            wrapper.className = 'slide-container';

            if (file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
                const img = document.createElement('img');
                img.src = url;
                wrapper.appendChild(img);
            } else {
                const vid = document.createElement('video');
                vid.src = url;
                vid.controls = true;
                wrapper.appendChild(vid);
            }

            const badge = document.createElement('span');
            badge.className = 'slide-badge';
            badge.innerText = `${index + 1}/${selectedFiles.length}`;
            wrapper.appendChild(badge);

            const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
            removeBtn.innerText = '✕';
            removeBtn.className = 'remove-btn';
            removeBtn.onclick = () => removeFile(index);
            wrapper.appendChild(removeBtn);

            carousel.appendChild(wrapper);
        });

        updateInputFiles();
    }

    function removeFile(index) {
        selectedFiles.splice(index, 1);
        renderPreview();
    }

    function updateInputFiles() {
        const dataTransfer = new DataTransfer();
        selectedFiles.forEach(file => dataTransfer.items.add(file));
        document.getElementById('fileInput').files = dataTransfer.files;
    }

    function updateCount(el) {
        document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = el.value.length + ' / 2200';
    }

    document.getElementById('postForm').addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
        if (selectedFiles.length === 0) {
            e.preventDefault();
            alert('Please select at least one file');
        }
    });

    // FIX 2: The formdata event listener has been completely removed so it stops deleting files before submission
</script>
</body>
</html>

            width: 34px; height: 34px; border-radius: 50%; overflow: hidden;

            display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
            color: #fff; font-weight: 700; font-size: 13px; flex-shrink: 0;
        }
        .pp-av img { width:100%; height:100%; object-fit:cover; }
        .pp-owner { font-size: 14px; font-weight: 600; color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-close {
            margin-left: auto; background: none; border: none;
            color: #8e8e8e; font-size: 22px; cursor: pointer; line-height: 1;
        }
        .pp-close:hover { color: #f5f5f5; }

        /* Scroll */
        .pp-scroll { flex: 1 1 auto; overflow-y: auto; padding: 10px 14px; }
        .pp-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar { width: 4px; }
        .pp-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb { background: #333; border-radius: 2px; }

        /* Caption */
        .pp-caption { display: flex; gap: 10px; margin-bottom: 12px; padding-bottom: 10px; border-bottom: 1px solid #2a2a2a; }
        .pp-caption-text { font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.4; color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-caption-text strong { font-weight: 600; margin-right: 4px; }

        .pp-no-comments { color: #8e8e8e; font-size: 14px; text-align: center; padding: 20px 0; }

        /* Comment */
        .pp-c { display: flex; gap: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; }
        .pp-c-av {
            width: 30px; height: 30px; border-radius: 50%; overflow: hidden;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg,#f58529,#dd2a7b,#8134af);
            display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
            color: #fff; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 700; flex-shrink: 0;
        }
        .pp-c-av img { width:100%; height:100%; object-fit:cover; }
        .pp-c-body { flex: 1; min-width: 0; }
        .pp-c-text { font-size: 13.5px; line-height: 1.4; color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-c-text strong { font-weight: 600; margin-right: 4px; }
        .pp-c-meta { display: flex; gap: 10px; font-size: 11px; color: #8e8e8e; margin-top: 3px; flex-wrap: wrap; }
        .pp-reply-btn, .pp-del-btn {
            background: none; border: none; cursor: pointer;
            color: #8e8e8e; font-size: 11px; padding: 0;
        }
        .pp-reply-btn:hover { color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-del-btn { color: #ff4d4f; display: none; }
        .pp-del-btn.show { display: inline; }

        /* Replies */
        .pp-replies { margin-left: 40px; margin-top: 4px; padding-left: 8px; border-left: 2px solid #2a2a2a; }
        .pp-vr-btn {
            display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px; background: none; border: none;
            color: #8e8e8e; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 600; cursor: pointer; margin: 4px 0 4px 40px;
        }
        .pp-vr-btn::before { content:''; width:20px; height:1px; background:#8e8e8e; }
        .pp-vr-btn:hover { color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-vr-btn:hover::before { background: #f5f5f5; }

        /* Footer */
        .pp-footer { border-top: 1px solid #2a2a2a; flex-shrink: 0; }
        .pp-actions { display: flex; gap: 14px; padding: 8px 14px 4px; }
        .pp-act-btn {
            background: none; border: none; cursor: pointer;
            color: #f5f5f5; font-size: 22px; padding: 0;
            transition: transform .15s;
        }
        .pp-act-btn:hover { transform: scale(1.12); }
        .pp-like-count { font-size: 14px; font-weight: 600; padding: 0 14px 2px; color: #f5f5f5; }
        .pp-time { font-size: 10px; color: #8e8e8e; padding: 0 14px 8px; text-transform: uppercase; letter-spacing: .4px; }

        /* Reply banner */
        .pp-reply-bar {
            display: none; align-items: center; justify-content: space-between;
            padding: 5px 14px; background: #1a1a1a; font-size: 12px; color: #8e8e8e;
            border-top: 1px solid #2a2a2a;
        }
        .pp-reply-bar.on { display: flex; }
        .pp-cancel-reply { background: none; border: none; color: #8e8e8e; cursor: pointer; font-size: 14px; }

        /* Input */
        .pp-input-row {
            display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px;
            padding: 8px 14px; border-top: 1px solid #2a2a2a;
        }
        .pp-input {
            flex: 1; border: none; outline: none; font-size: 14px;
            background: transparent; color: #f5f5f5; font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        }
        .pp-input::placeholder { color: #8e8e8e; }
        .pp-post-btn {
            background: none; border: none; color: #0095f6;
            font-weight: 700; cursor: pointer; font-size: 14px; font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
        }
        .pp-post-btn:disabled { opacity: .4; cursor: default; }

        /* Spinner */
        .pp-spin-wrap { display: flex; justify-content: center; padding: 40px 0; }
        .pp-spinner {
            width: 30px; height: 30px; border: 3px solid #333;
            border-top-color: #fff; border-radius: 50%;
            animation: ppSpin .7s linear infinite;
        }
        @keyframes ppSpin { to{transform:rotate(360deg)} }

        @media(max-width:768px){
            .pp-overlay { padding: 0; }
            .pp-card { flex-direction: column; border-radius: 0; max-height: 100vh; }
            .pp-left { flex: 0 0 50vw; }
            .pp-right { flex: 1 1 auto; width: 100%; border-left: none; border-top: 1px solid #2a2a2a; }
        }
    </style>
</head>

            <input type="text" id="searchInput" placeholder="Search" autocomplete="off"/>
        </div>
        <div class="search-dropdown" id="searchDropdown"></div>
    </div>

    <div class="nav-icons" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:20px;font-size:24px;">
        <a th:href="@{/posts}" title="Home" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">
            <i class="fa-solid fa-house"></i>
        </a>
        <a th:href="@{/posts/new}" title="New Post" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">
            <i class="fa-regular fa-square-plus"></i>
        </a>
        <a th:href="@{/users/{id}/profile(id=${currentUser.id})}" title="Profile" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">
            <i class="fa-regular fa-circle-user"></i>
        </a>
        <form th:action="@{/logout}" method="post" style="display:inline;margin:0;">
            <button type="submit" title="Logout" style="background:none;border:none;padding:0;cursor:pointer;color:inherit;font-size:24px;">
                <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right-from-bracket"></i>
            </button>
        </form>
    </div>

<div class="layout">
    <main>
        <div class="post-card" th:each="post : ${posts}">
            <div class="post-header">
                <a class="post-user" th:href="@{/users/{id}/profile(id=${post.user.id})}">
                    <div class="post-avatar">
                        <img th:if="${post.user.profilePicUrl != null}"
                             th:src="${post.user.profilePicUrl}"
                             th:alt="${post.user.username}"
                             style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:50%;border:1.5px solid #000;"/>
                        <div class="post-avatar-inner"
                             th:unless="${post.user.profilePicUrl != null}"
                             th:text="${not #strings.isEmpty(post.user.username) ? #strings.substring(post.user.username,0,1).toUpperCase() : '?'}">A</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-username" th:text="${post.user.username}">username</div>
                </a>

                <button th:if="${post.user.id == currentUser.id}"
                        class="post-more"
                        th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}"
                        onclick="openDeleteModal(this)" title="Delete">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-trash-can"></i>
                </button>
            </div>

            <div class="post-carousel-container" style="display:flex;overflow-x:auto;scroll-snap-type:x mandatory;scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;">
                <div th:each="media, mediaStat : ${post.carouselMedia}" class="carousel-slide" style="flex:0 0 100%;scroll-snap-align:start;position:relative;">
                    <img th:if="${media.mediaType == 'IMAGE'}"
                         th:src="${media.mediaUrl}"
                         style="width:100%;height:auto;max-height:600px;object-fit:cover;display:block;"
                         th:alt="${post.caption}"/>
                    <video th:if="${media.mediaType == 'VIDEO'}"
                           th:src="${media.mediaUrl}" controls
                           style="width:100%;height:auto;max-height:600px;object-fit:cover;display:block;"></video>
                    <div th:if="${#lists.size(post.carouselMedia) > 1}"
                         style="position:absolute;top:10px;right:10px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.6);color:white;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:12px;font-size:12px;z-index:10;">
                        <span th:text="${mediaStat.count}"></span> / <span th:text="${#lists.size(post.carouselMedia)}"></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="post-actions">
                <!-- Like -->
                <button class="action-btn like-btn"
                        th:with="isLiked=${post.likes != null and #lists.contains(post.likes.![user.id], currentUser.id)}"
                        th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}, data-liked=${isLiked}"
                        style="background:none;border:none;padding:0;cursor:pointer;margin-right:12px;" title="Like">
                    <i class="fa-heart like-icon"
                       th:classappend="${isLiked} ? 'fa-solid' : 'fa-regular'"
                       style="font-size:24px;"></i>
                </button>

                <!--
                    FIX: was <a href="/posts/{id}"> which causes full page navigation.
                    Changed to a button that opens the popup via JS.
                -->
                <button class="action-btn"
                        th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}"
                        onclick="openPostPopup(this.dataset.postId)"
                        style="background:none;border:none;padding:0;cursor:pointer;color:inherit;margin-right:12px;" title="Comment">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-comment" style="font-size:24px;"></i>
                </button>

                <button class="action-btn" title="Share" style="background:none;border:none;padding:0;cursor:pointer;color:inherit;">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-paper-plane" style="font-size:24px;"></i>
                </button>
            </div>

            <div class="likes-count">
                <span th:id="'like-count-' + ${post.id}"
                      th:with="lCount=${post.likes != null ? #lists.size(post.likes) : 0}"
                      th:text="${lCount} + ' ' + (${lCount} == 1 ? 'like' : 'likes')"></span>
            </div>

            <div class="post-caption">
                <span class="cap-username" th:text="${post.user.username}">username</span>
                <span th:text="${post.caption}">Caption here</span>
            </div>

            <!--
                FIX: was <a href="/posts/{id}"> — now opens popup instead.
            -->
            <button class="view-comments"
                    th:if="${not #lists.isEmpty(post.comments)}"
                    th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}"
                    onclick="openPostPopup(this.dataset.postId)"
                    th:text="'View all ' + ${#lists.size(post.comments)} + ' comment' + (${#lists.size(post.comments) > 1} ? 's' : '')">
                View all comments
            </button>

            <div class="post-time" th:text="${post.createdAt}">2 hours ago</div>

            <!--
                Inline quick-comment bar on the feed card.
                FIX: intercept submit via JS → POST JSON to /posts/comments/add
                → no page reload. If JS fails it falls back to normal form submit.
            -->
            <form class="post-comment-bar feed-comment-form"
                  th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}, data-user-id=${currentUser.id}"
                  onsubmit="return feedSubmitComment(event, this)">
                <span style="font-size:18px">&#128512;</span>
                <input class="comment-input feed-comment-input" type="text"
                       placeholder="Add a comment…" autocomplete="off"/>
                <button type="submit" class="post-btn">Post</button>
            </form>
        </div>
    </main>
</div>

<!-- Delete post modal -->
<div class="modal-overlay" id="deleteModal">
    <div class="modal-box">
        <div class="modal-title">Delete post?</div>
        <div class="modal-subtitle">Are you sure you want to delete this post?</div>
        <form id="deleteForm" method="post">
            <button type="submit" class="modal-btn delete">Delete</button>
        </form>
        <button class="modal-btn cancel" onclick="closeDeleteModal()">Cancel</button>
    </div>
</div>

<!-- ── Post popup (injected by JS) ── -->
<div id="ppOverlay" class="pp-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)closePP()">
    <div class="pp-card">
        <div class="pp-left" id="ppLeft">
            <button class="pp-nav pp-prev" onclick="ppNav(-1)">&#8249;</button>
            <div id="ppMedia" style="width:100%;height:100%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;"></div>
            <button class="pp-nav pp-next" onclick="ppNav(1)">&#8250;</button>
            <div class="pp-dots" id="ppDots"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="pp-right">
            <div class="pp-header">
                <div class="pp-av" id="ppAv"></div>
                <span class="pp-owner" id="ppOwner"></span>
                <button class="pp-close" onclick="closePP()"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark"></i></button>
            </div>
            <div class="pp-scroll" id="ppScroll">
                <div class="pp-spin-wrap"><div class="pp-spinner"></div></div>
            </div>
            <div class="pp-footer">
                <div class="pp-actions">
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" id="ppLikeBtn" onclick="ppLike()" title="Like">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-heart" id="ppLikeIcon"></i>
                    </button>
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" onclick="document.getElementById('ppInput').focus()" title="Comment">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-comment"></i>
                    </button>
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" title="Share">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-paper-plane"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="pp-like-count" id="ppLikeCount"></div>
                <div class="pp-time" id="ppTime"></div>
                <div class="pp-reply-bar" id="ppReplyBar">
                    <span>Replying to <strong id="ppReplyLabel"></strong></span>
                    <button class="pp-cancel-reply" onclick="ppCancelReply()">&#10005;</button>
                </div>
                <div class="pp-input-row">
                    <input class="pp-input" id="ppInput" type="text"
                           placeholder="Add a comment…" autocomplete="off"
                           oninput="document.getElementById('ppPostBtn').disabled=!this.value.trim()"/>
                    <button class="pp-post-btn" id="ppPostBtn" disabled onclick="ppSubmit()">Post</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script th:inline="javascript">
    /* ── CSRF helpers ── */
    const csrfToken  = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf"]').getAttribute('content');
    const csrfHeader = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf_header"]').getAttribute('content');
    const currentUserId = /*[[${currentUser.id}]]*/ null;

    function secureHeaders(json) {
        const h = { [csrfHeader]: csrfToken };
        if (json) h['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
        return h;
    }

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       FEED INLINE COMMENT (no reload)
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    function feedSubmitComment(e, form) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const input   = form.querySelector('.feed-comment-input');
        const content = input.value.trim();
        if (!content) return false;

        const postId = form.dataset.postId;
        const userId = form.dataset.userId;

        fetch('/posts/comments/add', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: secureHeaders(true),
            body: JSON.stringify({ postId: parseInt(postId), userId: parseInt(userId), content })
        })
        .then(r => r.json())
        .then(() => { input.value = ''; })
        .catch(console.error);

        return false;
    }

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       POST POPUP
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    let ppMediaList = [], ppMediaIdx = 0, ppPostId = null, ppReplyId = null;

    function openPostPopup(postId) {
        ppPostId  = postId;
        ppMediaList = []; ppMediaIdx = 0; ppReplyId = null;

        document.getElementById('ppOverlay').classList.add('pp-open');
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        document.getElementById('ppScroll').innerHTML =
            '<div class="pp-spin-wrap"><div class="pp-spinner"></div></div>';

        fetch('/posts/' + postId + '/data')
            .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error(r.status); return r.json(); })
            .then(renderPopup)
            .catch(err => {
                document.getElementById('ppScroll').innerHTML =
                    '<p style="color:#e1306c;padding:20px;text-align:center;">Failed to load post.</p>';
                console.error(err);
            });
    }

    function closePP() {
        document.getElementById('ppOverlay').classList.remove('pp-open');
        document.body.style.overflow = '';
        ppPostId = null; ppReplyId = null;
        ppCancelReply();
    }

    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closePP(); });

    /* ── Render ── */
    function renderPopup(d) {
        ppMediaList = d.media || [];
        ppMediaIdx  = 0;
        renderMedia();

        // Avatar
        const av = document.getElementById('ppAv');
        if (d.user.profilePicUrl) {
            av.innerHTML = `<img src="${esc(d.user.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/>`;
        } else {
            av.textContent = (d.user.username || '?').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
        }
        document.getElementById('ppOwner').textContent = d.user.username;

        renderLike(d.liked, d.likeCount);
        document.getElementById('ppTime').textContent = fmtDate(d.createdAt);
        renderComments(d);
    }

    /* ── Media carousel ── */
    function renderMedia() {
        const wrap = document.getElementById('ppMedia');
        const dots = document.getElementById('ppDots');
        const prev = document.querySelector('.pp-prev');
        const next = document.querySelector('.pp-next');
        const m = ppMediaList[ppMediaIdx];
        if (!m) { wrap.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#8e8e8e">No media</p>'; return; }

        if (m.mediaType === 'IMAGE') {
            wrap.innerHTML = `<img src="${esc(m.mediaUrl)}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:contain;" alt=""/>`;
        } else {
            wrap.innerHTML = `<video src="${esc(m.mediaUrl)}" controls style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:contain;"></video>`;
        }

        dots.innerHTML = '';
        ppMediaList.forEach((_, i) => {
            const d = document.createElement('div');
            d.className = 'pp-dot' + (i === ppMediaIdx ? ' active' : '');
            d.onclick = () => { ppMediaIdx = i; renderMedia(); };
            dots.appendChild(d);
        });

        prev.style.display = ppMediaList.length > 1 && ppMediaIdx > 0  ? 'flex' : 'none';
        next.style.display = ppMediaList.length > 1 && ppMediaIdx < ppMediaList.length - 1 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }

    function ppNav(dir) {
        const ni = ppMediaIdx + dir;
        if (ni < 0 || ni >= ppMediaList.length) return;
        ppMediaIdx = ni; renderMedia();
    }

    /* ── Like ── */
    function renderLike(liked, count) {
        const icon = document.getElementById('ppLikeIcon');
        icon.className = liked ? 'fa-solid fa-heart' : 'fa-regular fa-heart';
        icon.style.color = liked ? '#ff3040' : '';
        const el = document.getElementById('ppLikeCount');
        el.textContent = count > 0 ? count + (count === 1 ? ' like' : ' likes') : '';
    }

    function ppLike() {
        if (!ppPostId) return;
        fetch('/posts/' + ppPostId + '/like', { method: 'POST', headers: secureHeaders(false) })
            .then(r => r.json())
            .then(d => renderLike(d.liked, d.likeCount))
            .catch(console.error);
    }

    /* ── Comments ── */
    function renderComments(d) {
        const scroll = document.getElementById('ppScroll');
        scroll.innerHTML = '';

        if (d.caption) {
            const cap = document.createElement('div');
            cap.className = 'pp-caption';
            cap.innerHTML = buildAvHtml(d.user) +
                `<div class="pp-caption-text"><strong>${esc(d.user.username)}</strong>${esc(d.caption)}</div>`;
            scroll.appendChild(cap);
        }

        if (!d.comments || d.comments.length === 0) {
            scroll.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', '<div class="pp-no-comments">No comments yet.</div>');
            return;
        }

        d.comments.forEach(c => scroll.appendChild(buildCEl(c)));
    }

    function buildAvHtml(u) {
        if (u.profilePicUrl) return `<div class="pp-c-av"><img src="${esc(u.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/></div>`;
        return `<div class="pp-c-av">${(u.username || '?').charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>`;
    }

    function buildCEl(c) {
        const isOwner = c.userId === currentUserId;
        const avHtml  = c.profilePicUrl
            ? `<div class="pp-c-av"><img src="${esc(c.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/></div>`
            : `<div class="pp-c-av">${(c.username || '?').charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>`;

        const el = document.createElement('div');
        el.className = 'pp-c';
        el.dataset.commentId = c.id;
        el.dataset.userId    = c.userId;

        el.innerHTML = `
            ${avHtml}
            <div class="pp-c-body">
              <div class="pp-c-text"><strong>${esc(c.username)}</strong>${esc(c.content)}</div>
              <div class="pp-c-meta">
                <span>${fmtDate(c.createdAt)}</span>
                <button class="pp-reply-btn" data-id="${c.id}" data-un="${esc(c.username)}">Reply</button>
                <button class="pp-del-btn ${isOwner ? 'show' : ''}" data-id="${c.id}">Delete</button>
              </div>
              ${c.replyCount > 0
                ? `<button class="pp-vr-btn" data-id="${c.id}" data-cnt="${c.replyCount}">
                     View ${c.replyCount} ${c.replyCount===1?'reply':'replies'}
                   </button>` : ''}
            </div>`;

        el.querySelector('.pp-reply-btn').onclick = function () {
            ppStartReply(this.dataset.id, this.dataset.un);
        };

        const db = el.querySelector('.pp-del-btn');
        if (db) db.onclick = function () { ppDelete(this.dataset.id, el); };

        const vr = el.querySelector('.pp-vr-btn');
        if (vr) vr.onclick = function () { ppToggleReplies(this, c.id); };

        return el;
    }

    /* ── Reply ── */
    function ppStartReply(id, username) {
        ppReplyId = id;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyLabel').textContent = '@' + username;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyBar').classList.add('on');
        const inp = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        inp.placeholder = 'Reply to @' + username + '…';
        inp.focus();
    }

    function ppCancelReply() {
        ppReplyId = null;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyBar').classList.remove('on');
        const inp = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        if (inp) { inp.placeholder = 'Add a comment…'; inp.value = ''; }
        const btn = document.getElementById('ppPostBtn');
        if (btn) btn.disabled = true;
    }

    /* ── Submit comment ── */
    function ppSubmit() {
        const inp     = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        const content = inp.value.trim();
        if (!content || !ppPostId) return;

        const body = {
            postId:   parseInt(ppPostId),
            content,
            parentId: ppReplyId ? parseInt(ppReplyId) : null,
            replyingToUsername: ppReplyId
                ? document.getElementById('ppReplyLabel').textContent.replace('@', '')
                : null
        };

        fetch('/posts/comments/add', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: secureHeaders(true),
            body: JSON.stringify(body)
        })
        .then(r => r.json())
        .then(nc => {
            inp.value = '';
            document.getElementById('ppPostBtn').disabled = true;
            const rid = ppReplyId;
            ppCancelReply();

            if (!nc) return;
            const scroll = document.getElementById('ppScroll');
            const noC = scroll.querySelector('.pp-no-comments');
            if (noC) noC.remove();

            if (rid) {
                    let rDiv = document.getElementById('pp-r-' + rid);

                    if (!rDiv) {
                        rDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        rDiv.className = 'pp-replies';
                        rDiv.id = 'pp-r-' + rid;

                        const parentEl = document.querySelector(`[data-comment-id="${rid}"] .pp-c-body`);
                        if (parentEl) parentEl.appendChild(rDiv);
                    }

                    rDiv.style.display = 'block';

                    const el = buildCEl(nc);

                    el.style.marginLeft = "0px";

                    rDiv.appendChild(el);
                }
             else {
                scroll.appendChild(buildCEl(nc));
                scroll.scrollTop = scroll.scrollHeight;
            }
        })
        .catch(console.error);
    }
    function flattenReplies(replies) {
    let result = [];

    function dfs(list) {
        list.forEach(r => {
            result.push(r);
            if (r.replies && r.replies.length) {
                dfs(r.replies);
            }
        });
    }

            dfs(replies);
            return result;
        }

    /* ── Toggle replies ── */
    function ppToggleReplies(btn, parentId) {
    const cont = document.getElementById('pp-r-' + parentId);
    if (!cont) return;

    if (cont.dataset.loaded === 'true') {
        const hidden = cont.style.display === 'none';
        cont.style.display = hidden ? 'block' : 'none';
        btn.innerHTML = hidden
            ? 'Hide replies'
            : 'View ' + btn.dataset.cnt + ' ' + (btn.dataset.cnt == 1 ? 'reply' : 'replies');
        return;
    }

    btn.textContent = 'Loading…';

    fetch('/comments/replies/' + parentId)
        .then(r => r.json())
        .then(replies => {

            cont.innerHTML = '';

            const flatReplies = flattenReplies(replies);

            flatReplies.forEach(r => {
                const el = buildCEl(r);

                el.style.marginLeft = "0px";

                cont.appendChild(el);
            });

            cont.dataset.loaded = 'true';
            cont.style.display  = 'block';
            btn.textContent = 'Hide replies';
        })
        .catch(() => {
            btn.textContent = 'View ' + btn.dataset.cnt + ' replies';
        });
}

    /* ── Delete comment ── */
    function ppDelete(id, el) {
        fetch('/comments/delete/' + id, { method: 'POST', headers: secureHeaders(false) })
            .then(r => { if (r.ok) { el.remove(); const rd = document.getElementById('pp-r-'+id); if(rd)rd.remove(); }
                         else alert('Could not delete comment.'); })
            .catch(console.error);
    }

    /* ── Helpers ── */
    function esc(s) {
        const d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML;
    }
    function fmtDate(iso) {
        if (!iso) return '';
        try { return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'}); }
        catch(e){ return ''; }
    }

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       DELETE POST MODAL
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    function openDeleteModal(btn) {
        const postId = btn.dataset.postId;
        const form   = document.getElementById('deleteForm');
        form.action  = '/posts/' + postId + '/delete';
        const old = form.querySelector('input[name="_csrf"]');
        if (old) old.remove();
        const ci = document.createElement('input');
        ci.type = 'hidden'; ci.name = '_csrf'; ci.value = csrfToken;
        form.appendChild(ci);
        document.getElementById('deleteModal').classList.add('active');
    }
    function closeDeleteModal() { document.getElementById('deleteModal').classList.remove('active'); }
    document.getElementById('deleteModal').addEventListener('click', e => { if(e.target===e.currentTarget) closeDeleteModal(); });

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       LIKE BUTTON (feed cards)
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    document.querySelectorAll('.like-btn').forEach(btn => {
        const icon = btn.querySelector('.like-icon');
        if (btn.dataset.liked === 'true') {
            icon.classList.replace('fa-regular','fa-solid'); icon.style.color = '#ff3040';
        }
        btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
            const pid = this.dataset.postId;
            fetch('/posts/' + pid + '/like', { method: 'POST', headers: secureHeaders(false) })
                .then(r => r.json())
                .then(data => {
                    if (data.liked) { icon.classList.replace('fa-regular','fa-solid'); icon.style.color='#ff3040'; }
                    else            { icon.classList.replace('fa-solid','fa-regular');  icon.style.color=''; }
                    const cnt = document.getElementById('like-count-'+pid);
                    if (cnt) cnt.textContent = data.likeCount + ' ' + (data.likeCount===1?'like':'likes');
                })
                .catch(console.error);
        });
    });

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       SEARCH
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    (function () {
        const input    = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        const dropdown = document.getElementById('searchDropdown');
        if (!input || !dropdown) return;
        let timer;
        input.addEventListener('input', function () {
            const q = this.value.trim();
            clearTimeout(timer); dropdown.innerHTML = '';
            if (!q) { dropdown.classList.remove('open'); return; }
            timer = setTimeout(() => {
                fetch('/users/search?query=' + encodeURIComponent(q), { headers: {'X-Requested-With':'XMLHttpRequest'} })
                    .then(r => r.json())
                    .then(users => {
                        dropdown.innerHTML = '';
                        if (!users.length) { dropdown.innerHTML = '<div class="search-no-results">No users found</div>'; }
                        else {
                            users.forEach(u => {
                                const a = document.createElement('a');
                                a.href = '/users/'+u.id+'/profile';
                                a.className = 'search-result-item';
                                a.innerHTML = `<div class="search-result-avatar"><div class="search-result-avatar-inner">${u.username.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div></div>
                                               <div><div class="search-result-username">${escHtml(u.username)}</div></div>`;
                                dropdown.appendChild(a);
                            });
                        }
                        dropdown.classList.add('open');
                    }).catch(()=>{});
            }, 300);
        });
        document.addEventListener('click', e => {
            if (!document.getElementById('searchWrap').contains(e.target)) dropdown.classList.remove('open');
        });
        function escHtml(s){ return s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
    })();
</script>
</body>
</html>

                      th:action="@{/comments/add}"
                      method="POST"
                      id="commentForm">

                    <input type="hidden" name="postId" th:value="${post.id}"/>
                    <input type="hidden" name="userId" th:value="${currentUser?.id}"/>
                    <input type="hidden" name="parentId" id="parentIdField" value=""/>
                    <input type="hidden" name="replyingToUsername" id="replyingToUsername" />

                    <input class="comment-input"
                           id="commentInput"

<script th:inline="javascript">
    const currentUserId = [[${currentUser?.id}]];

    // Helper functions to get the exact CSRF token and header name Spring Boot expects
    function getCsrfToken() {
        const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf"]');
        return meta ? meta.getAttribute('content') : '';
    }

    function getCsrfHeader() {
        const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf_header"]');
        return meta ? meta.getAttribute('content') : 'X-CSRF-TOKEN';
    }

    // Standard headers for all secure fetch requests
    function getSecureHeaders() {
        const headers = { 'Accept': 'application/json' };
        const token = getCsrfToken();
        const headerName = getCsrfHeader();
        if (token && headerName) {
            headers[headerName] = token;
        }
        return headers;
    }

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        initComments();

        const input = document.getElementById('commentInput');
        if (input) {
            input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = !this.value.trim();
            });
        }

        const likeForm = document.getElementById('likeForm');
        if (likeForm) {
            likeForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();

                fetch(this.action, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: getSecureHeaders()
                })
                .then(function(response) {
                    if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to like post");
                    return response.json();
                })
                .then(function(data) {
                    const icon = document.getElementById('likeIcon');
                    if (data.liked) {
                        icon.className = 'fa-solid fa-heart';
                        icon.style.color = '#ff3040';
                    } else {
                        icon.className = 'fa-regular fa-heart';
                        icon.style.color = '';
                    }

                    const countDisplay = document.getElementById('likeCountDisplay');
                    if (data.likeCount > 0) {
                        countDisplay.textContent = data.likeCount + (data.likeCount === 1 ? ' like' : ' likes');
                    } else {
                        countDisplay.textContent = '';
                    }
                })
                .catch(function(error) {
                    console.error("Like Error:", error);
                });
            });
        }
    });

    function initComments() {
        const list = document.getElementById('commentsList');
        if (!list) return;
        list.querySelectorAll('.comment-item').forEach(wireCommentItem);
    }

    function wireCommentItem(item) {
        const commentId = item.dataset.commentId;
        const userId = parseInt(item.dataset.userId);

        const deleteBtn = item.querySelector('.delete-btn');
        if (deleteBtn && userId === currentUserId) {
            deleteBtn.classList.add('visible');
            deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                handleDelete(commentId, item);
            });
        }

        const replyBtn = item.querySelector('.reply-btn');
        if (replyBtn) {
            replyBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                prepareReply(this.dataset.commentId, this.dataset.username);
            });
        }

        const viewRepliesBtn = item.querySelector('.view-replies-btn');
        if (viewRepliesBtn) {
            viewRepliesBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                toggleReplies(this, commentId);
            });
        }
    }

    function prepareReply(commentId, username) {
        let parentCommentId = commentId;
        const commentElement = document.querySelector('[data-comment-id="' + commentId + '"]');
        const parentContainer = commentElement.closest('.comment-item');

        if (parentContainer && parentContainer.closest('.replies-list')) {
            const mainComment = parentContainer.closest('.replies-list').id.split('-')[1];
            parentCommentId = mainComment;
        }

        document.getElementById('parentIdField').value = parentCommentId;
        document.getElementById('replyingToUsername').value = username;
        document.getElementById('reply-username-label').textContent = '@' + username;
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.add('active');

        const input = document.getElementById('commentInput');
        input.placeholder = 'Reply to @' + username + '…';
        input.focus();
    }

    function cancelReply() {
        document.getElementById('parentIdField').value = '';
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('reply-info').classList.add('hidden');

        const input = document.getElementById('commentInput');
        input.placeholder = 'Add a comment…';
        input.value = '';
        document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = true;
    }

    const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('cancel-reply-btn');
    if (cancelBtn) cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', cancelReply);

    function toggleReplies(btn, parentId) {
        const container = document.getElementById('replies-' + parentId);
        if (!container) return;

        if (container.dataset.loaded === 'true') {
            if (container.style.display === 'none') {
                container.style.display = 'block';
                btn.innerHTML = 'Hide replies';
            } else {
                container.style.display = 'none';
                const count = btn.dataset.replyCount;
                btn.innerHTML = 'View ' + count + ' replies';
            }
            return;
        }

        const originalText = btn.innerHTML;
        btn.textContent = 'Loading…';

        fetch('/comments/replies/' + parentId)
            .then(function (res) {
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Server returned " + res.status);
                return res.json();
            })
            .then(function (replies) {
                container.innerHTML = '';

                replies.forEach(function (reply) {
                    const replyEl = buildReplyElement(reply);
                    container.appendChild(replyEl);
                    wireCommentItem(replyEl);
                });

                container.dataset.loaded = 'true';
                container.style.display = 'block';
                btn.innerHTML = 'Hide replies';
            })
            .catch(function (err) {
                console.error("View Replies Error:", err);
                alert("Could not load replies. Check your backend terminal for errors!");
                btn.innerHTML = originalText; // Reset button text
            });
    }

    function buildReplyElement(reply) {
        const initial = reply.username ? reply.username.charAt(0).toUpperCase() : '?';

        // Failsafe check in case your CommentResponse DTO uses different field names (like reply.id instead of reply.userId)
        const authorId = reply.userId || reply.user_id || reply.id;
        const isOwner = authorId === currentUserId;

        const avatar = reply.profilePicUrl || reply.profilePictureUrl
            ? `<img src="${reply.profilePicUrl || reply.profilePictureUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;border-radius:50%;" />`
            : `<span>${initial}</span>`;

        const item = document.createElement('div');
        item.className = 'comment-item';
        item.dataset.commentId = reply.id;
        item.dataset.userId = authorId;
        item.dataset.replyCount = 0;

        item.innerHTML = `
            <div class="small-avatar">${avatar}</div>
            <div class="comment-body">
                <div class="comment-text">
                    <strong>${escapeHtml(reply.username)}</strong>
                    <span>${escapeHtml(reply.content)}</span>
                </div>
                <div class="comment-meta">
                    <span class="comment-time">${formatDate(reply.createdAt)}</span>
                    <button class="reply-btn"
                            data-comment-id="${reply.id}"
                            data-username="${escapeHtml(reply.username)}">Reply</button>
                    <button class="delete-btn ${isOwner ? 'visible' : ''}"
                            data-comment-id="${reply.id}">Delete</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        return item;
    }

    function handleDelete(commentId, itemElement) {
        if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to delete this comment?")) return;

        fetch('/comments/delete/' + commentId, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: getSecureHeaders()
        })
        .then(function (res) {
            if (res.ok) {
                itemElement.remove();
                const repliesContainer = document.getElementById('replies-' + commentId);
                if (repliesContainer) repliesContainer.remove();

                // Hide the "View replies" button if it exists
                const viewBtn = document.querySelector('.view-replies-btn[data-comment-id="' + commentId + '"]');
                if (viewBtn) viewBtn.remove();

                // Optional: reload the page to refresh comment counts
                // setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 300);
            } else {
                return res.text().then(text => { throw new Error(text) });
            }
        })
        .catch(function (err) {
            console.error("Delete Error:", err);
            alert('Could not delete comment: ' + err.message);
        });
    }

    function goBack(event) {
        if (event.target === event.currentTarget) {
            window.location.href = '/posts';
        }
    }

    function escapeHtml(str) {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.textContent = str || '';
        return div.innerHTML;
    }

    function formatDate(isoString) {
        if (!isoString) return '';
        try {
            const d = new Date(isoString);
            return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
        } catch (e) {
            return '';
        }
    }
</script>

</body>
</html>

    <title>Instagram · New Reel</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" th:href="@{/css/reel-create.css}"/>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Grand+Hotel&family=DM+Sans:wght@300;400;500;600&display=swap" rel="stylesheet"/>
</head>
<body>
<nav>
    <a class="nav-logo" th:href="@{/posts}">Instagram</a>
    <div style="font-size:16px; font-weight:600;">New Reel</div>
    <a class="nav-back" th:href="@{/posts}">✕</a>
</nav>

<div class="page">
    <div th:if="${error}" class="alert" style="color: red; padding: 10px; text-align: center;" th:text="${error}"></div>

    <form th:action="@{/reels/create}" method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data" id="reelForm">

        <div class="modal">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <span style="color:var(--muted); font-size:14px;"></span>
                <span class="modal-title">New Reel</span>
                <button type="submit" class="share-btn" id="shareBtn">Share</button>
            </div>

            <div class="upload-area" id="uploadArea" onclick="document.getElementById('videoInput').click()">
                <div class="upload-icon">🎬</div>
                <div class="upload-title">Drag your video here</div>
                <div class="upload-subtitle">Max. 1 video, up to 30 seconds</div>
                <button type="button" class="upload-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); document.getElementById('videoInput').click()">
                    Select from computer
                </button>
                <input type="file" id="videoInput" name="file" accept="video/*"
                       onchange="handleVideoSelect(this)" style="display: none;"/>
            </div>

            <div id="previewContainer" class="preview-container" style="display: none;">
                <div class="video-wrapper">
                    <video id="videoPreview" controls></video>
                    <button type="button" class="remove-video-btn" onclick="removeVideo()">✕</button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="details-section">
                <div class="user-row">
                    <div class="user-avatar">
                        <div class="user-avatar-inner">👤</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="user-name" th:text="${#authentication != null ? #authentication.name : 'username'}">username</div>
                </div>
                <textarea class="caption-input" name="caption"
                          placeholder="Write a caption for your Reel…" maxlength="2200"
                          oninput="updateCount(this)"></textarea>
                <div class="caption-footer">
                    <span class="char-count" id="charCount">0 / 2200</span>
                </div>
                <div class="duration-info" id="durationInfo" style="display: none;">
                    <span>Video duration: <strong id="videoDuration">0</strong>s / 30s</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </form>
</div>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        document.getElementById('shareBtn').disabled = true;
    });

    let selectedVideo = null;

    function handleVideoSelect(input) {
        const file = input.files[0];

        if (!file) {
            return;
        }

        // Check if it's a video file
        if (!file.type.startsWith('video/')) {
            alert('Please select a valid video file');
            input.value = '';
            return;
        }

        // Check file size (max 50MB as per application.properties)
        if (file.size > 50 * 1024 * 1024) {
            alert('Video file is too large. Maximum 50MB allowed.');
            input.value = '';
            return;
        }

        selectedVideo = file;
        input.value = '';

        renderVideoPreview();
    }

    function renderVideoPreview() {
        const area = document.getElementById('uploadArea');
        const previewContainer = document.getElementById('previewContainer');
        const videoPreview = document.getElementById('videoPreview');
        const durationInfo = document.getElementById('durationInfo');
        const shareBtn = document.getElementById('shareBtn');

        if (!selectedVideo) {
            area.style.display = 'flex';
            previewContainer.style.display = 'none';
            durationInfo.style.display = 'none';
            shareBtn.disabled = true;
            return;
        }

        area.style.display = 'none';
        previewContainer.style.display = 'block';
        durationInfo.style.display = 'block';

        const url = URL.createObjectURL(selectedVideo);
        videoPreview.src = url;

        // Check video duration when metadata is loaded
        videoPreview.onloadedmetadata = function() {
            const duration = Math.floor(videoPreview.duration);
            document.getElementById('videoDuration').textContent = duration;

            if (duration > 30) {
                document.getElementById('durationInfo').style.color = '#e1306c';
                shareBtn.disabled = true;
                alert('Video is too long! Maximum duration is 30 seconds.');
            } else {
                document.getElementById('durationInfo').style.color = '#8e8e8e';
                shareBtn.disabled = false;
                updateInputFile();
            }
        };
    }

    function removeVideo() {
        selectedVideo = null;
        document.getElementById('videoInput').value = '';
        renderVideoPreview();
    }

    function updateInputFile() {
        if (!selectedVideo) {
            return;
        }

        const dataTransfer = new DataTransfer();
        dataTransfer.items.add(selectedVideo);
        document.getElementById('videoInput').files = dataTransfer.files;
    }

    function updateCount(el) {
        document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = el.value.length + ' / 2200';
    }

    document.getElementById('reelForm').addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
        if (!selectedVideo) {
            e.preventDefault();
            alert('Please select a video to upload');
            return;
        }

        const videoElement = document.getElementById('videoPreview');
        if (videoElement.duration > 30) {
            e.preventDefault();
            alert('Video exceeds 30 second limit');
            return;
        }
    });

    // Handle drag and drop
    const uploadArea = document.getElementById('uploadArea');
    
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.style.background = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)';
    });

    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
        uploadArea.style.background = '';
    });

    uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        uploadArea.style.background = '';
        
        const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
        if (files.length > 0) {
            document.getElementById('videoInput').files = files;
            handleVideoSelect(document.getElementById('videoInput'));
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

<div class="reel-page-container">
    <div class="reel-main">

        <!-- VIDEO -->
        <div class="reel-video-section">
            <video id="reelVideo" autoplay loop playsinline
                   th:src="${reel.videoUrl}" class="reel-video"></video>
        </div>

        <!-- SIDEBAR -->
        <div class="reel-sidebar">

            <div class="reel-user-card">

                     th:src="${reel.user.profilePicUrl != null ? reel.user.profilePicUrl : 'https://cdn-icons-png.flaticon.com/512/149/149071.png'}">
                <span class="username" th:text="${reel.user.username}"></span>

                <span th:text="${reel.caption}"></span>
            </div>

            <div class="reel-stats">
                <span class="stat-value" th:text="${reel.likeCount}">0</span>
                <span class="stat-value" th:text="${reel.commentCount}">0</span>
                <span class="stat-value" th:text="${reel.viewCount}">0</span>
            </div>

            <div class="reel-actions">
                <button type="button" id="likeBtn">♡</button>
                <button type="button" id="commentBtn">💬</button>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>

<div id="commentModal" class="comment-modal hidden">
    <div class="comment-box">

        <div class="comment-header">Comments</div>

        <div id="commentList" class="comment-list"></div>

        <div class="comment-input-bar">
            <input id="commentInput" placeholder="Add a comment..." />
            <button type="button" id="postCommentBtn">Post</button>
        </div>

    </div>
</div>

<!-- 🔥 IMPORTANT: inject userId correctly -->
<script th:inline="javascript">
    const userId = [[${currentUser.id}]];
</script>

<script>
    function getCsrfToken() {
     const match = document.cookie
         .split('; ')
         .find(row => row.startsWith('XSRF-TOKEN='));
     if (!match) return '';
     return decodeURIComponent(match.split('=')[1]);
 }

     document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {

         const reelId = parseInt(window.location.pathname.split('/').pop());

         const statValues = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-value');
         const likeStat = statValues[0];
         const commentStat = statValues[1];
         const viewStat = statValues[2];

         const likeBtn = document.getElementById('likeBtn');
         const commentBtn = document.getElementById('commentBtn');
         const modal = document.getElementById('commentModal');
         const commentList = document.getElementById('commentList');
         const input = document.getElementById('commentInput');
         const postBtn = document.getElementById('postCommentBtn');
         const video = document.getElementById('reelVideo');

         let isLiked = false;

         // ---------------- VIEW ----------------
         try {
             const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/view`, {
                 method: 'POST',
                 headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken() }
             });
             if (res.ok) viewStat.textContent = await res.text();
         } catch {}

         // ---------------- LIKE STATE ----------------
         try {
             const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/liked`);
             if (res.ok) {
                 isLiked = await res.json();
                 likeBtn.textContent = isLiked ? '❤️' : '♡';
             }
         } catch {}

         // ---------------- LIKE ----------------
         likeBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
             try {
                 const url = isLiked
                     ? `/reels/${reelId}/unlike`
                     : `/reels/${reelId}/like`;

                 const res = await fetch(url, {
                     method: 'POST',
                     headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken() }
                 });

                 if (!res.ok) throw new Error();

                 const count = await res.text();

                 isLiked = !isLiked;
                 likeBtn.textContent = isLiked ? '❤️' : '♡';
                 likeStat.textContent = count;

             } catch (e) {
                 console.error(e);
             }
         });

         // ---------------- VIDEO ----------------
         video.addEventListener('click', () => {
             video.paused ? video.play() : video.pause();
         });

         // ---------------- OPEN COMMENTS ----------------
         commentBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
             modal.classList.remove('hidden');

             try {
                 const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/comments`);
                 const comments = await res.json();

                 commentList.innerHTML = '';

                 if (!comments.length) {
                     commentList.innerHTML = '<div>No comments yet</div>';
                     return;
                 }

                 comments.forEach(c => {
                     commentList.innerHTML += `
                         <div class="comment-item">
                             <b>${c.username}</b>
                             <span>${c.content}</span>
                         </div>
                     `;
                 });

             } catch (e) {
                 console.error(e);
             }
         });

         // ---------------- CLOSE ----------------
         modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
             if (e.target === modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
         });

         // ---------------- POST COMMENT ----------------
         async function postComment() {
             const content = input.value.trim();
             if (!content) return;

             try {
                 const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/comments`, {
                     method: 'POST',
                     headers: {
                         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                         'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken()
                     },
                     body: JSON.stringify({
                         reelId: reelId,
                         userId: userId,
                         content: content
                     })
                 });

                 if (!res.ok) throw new Error();

                 const newComment = await res.json();

                 commentList.innerHTML =
                     `<div class="comment-item">
                         <b>${newComment.username}</b>
                         <span>${newComment.content}</span>
                     </div>`
                     + commentList.innerHTML;

                 input.value = '';

                 commentStat.textContent =
                     parseInt(commentStat.textContent || 0) + 1;

             } catch (e) {
                 console.error(e);
             }
         }

         postBtn.addEventListener('click', postComment);

         input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
             if (e.key === 'Enter') postComment();
         });

     });
</script>

</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html xmlns:th="http://www.thymeleaf.org" lang="en">
