    <meta charset="UTF-8"/>
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"/>
    <title>Instagram · Reels</title>
    <link rel="icon" href="data:,">
    <link rel="stylesheet" th:href="@{/css/reel-list.css}"/>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Grand+Hotel&family=DM+Sans:wght@300;400;500;600&display=swap" rel="stylesheet"/>
    <link href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.5.0/css/all.min.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
</head>
<body>

<nav class="nav-bar">
    <a class="nav-logo" th:href="@{/posts}">Instagram</a>
    <div class="nav-title">Reels</div>
</nav>

<div class="reels-container">

    <div th:if="${#lists.isEmpty(reels)}" class="no-reels-message">
        <h2>No Reels Yet</h2>
        <a th:href="@{/reels/create}">Create One</a>
    </div>

    <div th:each="reel : ${reels}" class="reel">

        <!-- reel-card clips all overlays inside the rounded video rectangle -->
        <div class="reel-card">

            <video class="reel-video" th:data-id="${reel.id}" muted loop playsinline>
                <source th:src="${reel.videoUrl}" type="video/mp4">
            </video>

            <!-- BOTTOM LEFT: username, caption, delete -->
            <div class="reel-left">
                <div class="username" th:text="${reel.user.username}">username</div>
                <div class="caption" th:text="${reel.caption}">caption</div>
                <button th:if="${currentUser != null and reel.user.id == currentUser.id}"
                        class="delete-reel-btn"
                        th:data-reel-id="${reel.id}">
                    🗑 Delete Reel
                </button>
            </div>

            <!-- BOTTOM RIGHT: like, comment, views -->
            <div class="reel-right">
                <div class="action like-btn" th:data-id="${reel.id}">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-heart"></i>
                    <span th:text="${reel.likeCount}">0</span>
                </div>
                <div class="action comment-btn" th:data-id="${reel.id}">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-comment"></i>
                    <span th:text="${reel.commentCount}">0</span>
                </div>
                <div class="action view-count">
                    <i class="fa-regular fa-eye"></i>
                    <span th:text="${reel.viewCount}">0</span>
                </div>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>

</div>

<!-- COMMENT MODAL -->
<div id="commentModal" class="comment-modal hidden">
    <div class="comment-sheet">
        <div class="comment-header">Comments</div>
        <div id="commentList" class="comment-list"></div>
        <div id="replyIndicator" class="reply-indicator">
            <span id="replyingToLabel"></span>
            <button id="cancelReply">✕</button>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-input-bar">
            <input id="commentInput" placeholder="Add a comment..." />
            <button id="postComment">Post</button>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script th:inline="javascript">
    const currentUserId = [[${currentUser != null ? currentUser.id : null}]];
</script>

<script>
    const DEFAULT_AVATAR = 'https://cdn-icons-png.flaticon.com/512/149/149071.png';

    function getCsrfToken() {
        const match = document.cookie.split('; ').find(r => r.startsWith('XSRF-TOKEN='));
        return match ? decodeURIComponent(match.split('=')[1]) : '';
    }

    function escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return str.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
    }

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {

        const csrfToken       = getCsrfToken();
        const modal           = document.getElementById('commentModal');
        const commentList     = document.getElementById('commentList');
        const input           = document.getElementById('commentInput');
        const postBtn         = document.getElementById('postComment');
        const replyIndicator  = document.getElementById('replyIndicator');
        const replyingToLabel = document.getElementById('replyingToLabel');
        const cancelReplyBtn  = document.getElementById('cancelReply');

        let currentReelId = null;
        let replyingTo    = null;

        /* ── DELETE REEL ── */
        document.querySelectorAll('.delete-reel-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                const reelId = btn.dataset.reelId;
                if (!confirm('Delete this reel? This cannot be undone.')) return;
                try {
                    const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}`, {
                        method: 'DELETE',
                        headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken() }
                    });
                    if (res.ok || res.redirected) {
                        btn.closest('.reel').remove();
                    } else {
                        alert('Failed to delete reel.');
                    }
                } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
            });
        });

        /* ── LIKE ── */
        document.querySelectorAll('.like-btn').forEach(async (btn) => {
            const reelId = btn.dataset.id;
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/liked`);
                if (res.ok && await res.json()) btn.classList.add('liked');
            } catch {}

            btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                const liked = btn.classList.contains('liked');
                try {
                    const res = await fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/${liked ? 'unlike' : 'like'}`, {
                        method: 'POST', headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': csrfToken }
                    });
                    btn.querySelector('span').textContent = await res.text();
                    btn.classList.toggle('liked');
                } catch {}
            });
        });

        /* ── OPEN COMMENTS ── */
        document.querySelectorAll('.comment-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                currentReelId = btn.dataset.id;
                modal.classList.remove('hidden');
                commentList.innerHTML = 'Loading...';
                clearReply();
                try {
                    const res      = await fetch(`/reels/${currentReelId}/comments`);
                    const comments = await res.json();
                    if (!comments.length) {
                        commentList.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-comments">No comments yet</div>';
                        return;
                    }
                    renderComments(comments);
                } catch {
                    commentList.innerHTML = 'Failed to load';
                }
            });
        });

        /* ── RENDER ── */
        function renderComments(comments) {
            commentList.innerHTML = comments.map(c => buildCommentHTML(c)).join('');
            attachListeners();
        }

        function buildCommentHTML(c) {
            const avatar     = c.profilePicUrl || DEFAULT_AVATAR;
            const isOwn      = currentUserId !== null && c.userId === currentUserId;
            const hasReplies = c.replies && c.replies.length > 0;

            const rightAction = isOwn
                ? `<button class="delete-btn" data-comment-id="${c.id}">🗑</button>`
                : `<button class="follow-btn">Follow</button>`;

            const repliesSection = hasReplies ? `
                <button class="view-replies-btn" data-comment-id="${c.id}">
                    View ${c.replies.length} ${c.replies.length === 1 ? 'reply' : 'replies'}
                </button>
                <div class="replies-list hidden" id="replies-${c.id}">
                    ${c.replies.map(r => buildReplyHTML(r)).join('')}
                </div>` : '';

            return `
                <div class="comment-item" data-comment-id="${c.id}">
                    <img src="${avatar}" class="comment-avatar" onerror="this.src='${DEFAULT_AVATAR}'" />
                    <div class="comment-body">
                        <b>${escapeHtml(c.username)}</b><span>${escapeHtml(c.content)}</span>
                        <div class="comment-meta">
                            <button class="reply-btn"
                                data-username="${escapeHtml(c.username)}"
                                data-comment-id="${c.id}">Reply</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    ${rightAction}
                </div>
                ${repliesSection}
            `;
        }

        function buildReplyHTML(r) {
            const avatar = r.profilePicUrl || DEFAULT_AVATAR;
            const isOwn  = currentUserId !== null && r.userId === currentUserId;
            const deleteBtn = isOwn
                ? `<button class="delete-btn" data-comment-id="${r.id}">🗑</button>`
                : '';
            return `
                <div class="reply-item" data-comment-id="${r.id}">
                    <img src="${avatar}" class="reply-avatar" onerror="this.src='${DEFAULT_AVATAR}'" />
                    <div class="reply-body">
                        <b>${escapeHtml(r.username)}</b><span>${escapeHtml(r.content)}</span>
                    </div>
                    ${deleteBtn}
                </div>
            `;
        }

        function attachListeners() {
            commentList.querySelectorAll('.reply-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    replyingTo = { commentId: btn.dataset.commentId, username: btn.dataset.username };
                    replyingToLabel.innerHTML = `Replying to <b>@${escapeHtml(btn.dataset.username)}</b>`;
                    replyIndicator.classList.add('visible');
                    input.placeholder = `Reply to @${btn.dataset.username}...`;
                    input.focus();
                });
            });

            commentList.querySelectorAll('.view-replies-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const div    = document.getElementById(`replies-${btn.dataset.commentId}`);
                    const hidden = div.classList.toggle('hidden');
                    const count  = div.querySelectorAll('.reply-item').length;
                    btn.textContent = hidden
                        ? `View ${count} ${count === 1 ? 'reply' : 'replies'}`
                        : 'Hide replies';
                });
            });

            commentList.querySelectorAll('.follow-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const following = btn.textContent === 'Following';
                    btn.textContent = following ? 'Follow'  : 'Following';
                    btn.style.color = following ? '#0095f6' : '#a8a8a8';
                });
            });

            commentList.querySelectorAll('.delete-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                    const commentId = btn.dataset.commentId;
                    if (!confirm('Delete this comment?')) return;

                    const commentEl = commentList.querySelector(`[data-comment-id="${commentId}"]`);
                    const isReply   = commentEl?.closest('.replies-list') !== null;

                    try {
                        const res = await fetch(`/reels/${currentReelId}/comments/${commentId}`, {
                            method: 'DELETE',
                            headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken() }
                        });
                        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);

                        if (commentEl) {
                            if (!isReply) {
                                const next = commentEl.nextElementSibling;
                                if (next?.classList?.contains('view-replies-btn')) {
                                    next.nextElementSibling?.remove();
                                    next.remove();
                                }
                            }
                            commentEl.remove();
                        }

                        if (!isReply) {
                            const card    = document.querySelector(`video[data-id='${currentReelId}']`).closest('.reel-card');
                            const countEl = card.querySelector('.comment-btn span');
                            const current = parseInt(countEl.textContent || '0');
                            if (current > 0) countEl.textContent = current - 1;
                        }
                    } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to delete comment:', e); }
                });
            });
        }

        /* ── CANCEL REPLY ── */
        cancelReplyBtn.addEventListener('click', clearReply);
        function clearReply() {
            replyingTo = null;
            replyIndicator.classList.remove('visible');
            input.placeholder = 'Add a comment...';
        }

        /* ── POST ── */
        postBtn.addEventListener('click', postComment);
        input.addEventListener('keypress', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') postComment(); });

        async function postComment() {
            const text = input.value.trim();
            if (!text) return;

            const payload = { reelId: parseInt(currentReelId), content: text };
            if (replyingTo) {
                payload.parentId = parseInt(replyingTo.commentId);
                payload.replyingToUsername = replyingTo.username;
            }

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/reels/${currentReelId}/comments`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': getCsrfToken() },
                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
                });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
                const c = await res.json();

                if (replyingTo) {
                    const parentId = replyingTo.commentId;
                    let repliesDiv = document.getElementById(`replies-${parentId}`);
                    if (!repliesDiv) {
                        const parentItem = commentList.querySelector(`.comment-item[data-comment-id="${parentId}"]`);
                        parentItem.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', `
                            <button class="view-replies-btn" data-comment-id="${parentId}">Hide replies</button>
                            <div class="replies-list" id="replies-${parentId}"></div>
                        `);
                        repliesDiv = document.getElementById(`replies-${parentId}`);
                        attachListeners();
                    } else {
                        repliesDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
                        const toggleBtn = commentList.querySelector(`.view-replies-btn[data-comment-id="${parentId}"]`);
                        if (toggleBtn) toggleBtn.textContent = 'Hide replies';
                    }
                    repliesDiv.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', buildReplyHTML(c));
                    attachListeners();
                    clearReply();
                } else {
                    commentList.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', buildCommentHTML(c));
                    attachListeners();
                    const card    = document.querySelector(`video[data-id='${currentReelId}']`).closest('.reel-card');
                    const countEl = card.querySelector('.comment-btn span');
                    countEl.textContent = parseInt(countEl.textContent || '0') + 1;
                }
                input.value = '';
            } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to post comment:', e); }
        }

        /* ── CLOSE ── */
        modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target === modal) { modal.classList.add('hidden'); clearReply(); }
        });

        /* ── VIEW ── */
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                const video  = entry.target;
                const reelId = video.dataset.id;
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    video.play().catch(() => {});
                    if (!video.dataset.viewed) {
                        video.dataset.viewed = 'true';
                        fetch(`/reels/${reelId}/view`, {
                            method: 'POST', headers: { 'X-XSRF-TOKEN': csrfToken }
                        }).then(r => r.text()).then(count => {
                            video.closest('.reel-card').querySelector('.view-count span').textContent = count;
                        });
                    }
                } else {
                    video.pause();
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.7 });

        document.querySelectorAll('.reel-video').forEach(v => observer.observe(v));
    });
</script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
    // Init bio count on load
    const bioArea = document.querySelector('textarea[name="bio"]');
    if (bioArea) {
        document.getElementById('bioCount').textContent = bioArea.value.length + ' / 150';
    }
    function updateBioCount(el) {
        document.getElementById('bioCount').textContent = el.value.length + ' / 150';
    }

    /* ── URL validation ── */
    function validateUrl(input) {
        const val = input.value.trim();
        const errorEl = document.getElementById('urlErrorInline');
        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('urlClearBtn');

        clearBtn.style.display = val.length > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';

        if (val.length === 0) {
            errorEl.style.display = 'none';
            input.classList.remove('input-error');
            return;
        }

        const testVal = val.startsWith('http://') || val.startsWith('https://')
            ? val : 'https://' + val;

        try {
            const url = new URL(testVal);
            const valid = url.hostname.includes('.');
            errorEl.style.display = valid ? 'none' : 'flex';
            input.classList.toggle('input-error', !valid);
        } catch {
            errorEl.style.display = 'flex';
            input.classList.add('input-error');
        }
    }

    function clearUrl() {
        const input = document.getElementById('websiteInput');
        input.value = '';
        input.classList.remove('input-error');
        document.getElementById('urlErrorInline').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('urlClearBtn').style.display = 'none';
        input.focus();
    }

    // Init clear button visibility on load
    (function() {
        const input = document.getElementById('websiteInput');
        if (input && input.value.trim().length > 0) {
            document.getElementById('urlClearBtn').style.display = 'flex';
        }
    })();

    document.getElementById('picInput').addEventListener('change', function () {
        const file = this.files[0];
        if (!file) return;

        const maxBytes = 5 * 1024 * 1024; // 5 MB in bytes
        if (file.size > maxBytes) {
            alert('This image is larger than 5 MB. Please choose a smaller file.');
            this.value = ''; // Reset the file input so they must pick again
            return;
        }

        const reader = new FileReader();

        reader.onload = function (e) {

            const preview = document.getElementById('avatarPreview');
            preview.src = e.target.result;
            preview.style.display = 'block';

            const letterFallback = document.getElementById('letterFallback');
            if (letterFallback) letterFallback.style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('previewLabel').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('uploadBtn').style.display = 'inline';
        };

        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

            animation: ppSpin .7s linear infinite;
        }
        @keyframes ppSpin { to{transform:rotate(360deg)} }
        @media(max-width:768px){
            .pp-overlay { padding: 0; }
            .pp-card { flex-direction: column; border-radius: 0; max-height: 100vh; }
            .pp-left { flex: 0 0 50vw; }
            .pp-right { flex: 1 1 auto; width: 100%; border-left: none; border-top: 1px solid #2a2a2a; }
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<nav>
    <a class="nav-logo" th:href="@{/posts}">Instagram</a>
    <div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:600;" th:text="${user.username}">username</div>

        <a th:href="@{/posts}" title="Home"><i class="fa-solid fa-house"></i></a>
        <form th:action="@{/logout}" method="post" style="display:inline">
            <button type="submit" title="Logout"><i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right-from-bracket"></i></button>
        </form>
    </div>
</nav>

<div class="page">
    <div class="profile-header">
        <div class="profile-avatar-wrap">
            <div class="profile-avatar-ring">
                <div class="profile-avatar-inner">
                    <img th:if="${user.profilePicUrl != null}" th:src="${user.profilePicUrl}" th:alt="${user.username}"/>
                    <span th:unless="${user.profilePicUrl != null}"
                          th:text="${#strings.substring(user.username,0,1).toUpperCase()}">A</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="profile-info">
            <div class="profile-top">
                <span class="profile-username" th:text="${user.username}">username</span>

                <div class="profile-actions" th:if="${currentUser.id == user.id}">
                    <a class="btn-edit" th:href="@{/users/{id}/edit(id=${user.id})}">Edit profile</a>
                    <form th:action="@{/users/{id}/delete(id=${user.id})}" method="post"
                          style="display:inline" onsubmit="return confirm('Delete account?')">
                        <button class="btn-danger" type="submit">Delete account</button>
                    </form>
                </div>

                <div th:if="${currentUser.id != user.id}">
                    <form th:action="@{/users/{id}/follow(id=${user.id})}" method="post" style="display:inline">
                        <button th:if="${isFollowing}"  type="submit" class="btn-edit">Following</button>
                        <button th:unless="${isFollowing}" type="submit" class="btn-follow">Follow</button>
                    </form>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="profile-stats">
                <div class="stat">
                    <span class="stat-num" th:text="${#lists.size(posts)}">0</span>
                    <span class="stat-label">posts</span>
                </div>
                <a class="stat stat-link" th:href="@{/users/{id}/followers(id=${user.id})}">
                    <span class="stat-num" th:text="${followersCount}">0</span>
                    <span class="stat-label">followers</span>
                </a>
                <a class="stat stat-link" th:href="@{/users/{id}/following(id=${user.id})}">
                    <span class="stat-num" th:text="${followingCount}">0</span>
                    <span class="stat-label">following</span>
                </a>
            </div>

            <div class="profile-bio">
                <div class="display-name" th:text="${user.username}">username</div>
                <div class="bio-text" id="bioText"
                     th:attr="data-bio=${user.bio != null && !#strings.isEmpty(user.bio) ? user.bio : ''}"></div>
                <a th:if="${user.websiteUrl != null && !#strings.isEmpty(user.websiteUrl)}"
                   th:href="${user.websiteUrl}"
                   th:text="${user.websiteUrl.replaceAll('https?://', '')}"
                   class="profile-website-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"></a>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="profile-tabs">
        <div class="tab active"><i class="fa-solid fa-table-cells"></i> Posts</div>
        <div class="tab"><i class="fa-solid fa-film"></i> Reels</div>
        <div class="tab"><i class="fa-regular fa-id-badge"></i> Tagged</div>
    </div>

    <div class="posts-grid">
        <div th:if="${#lists.isEmpty(posts)}" class="empty-grid">
            <div class="icon"><i class="fa-regular fa-image"></i></div>
            <h3>Share Photos</h3>
            <p>When you share photos, they will appear on your profile.</p>
            <a th:href="@{/posts/new}" class="create-btn">+ Share your first photo</a>

        <!--
            FIX: removed iframe approach (openPostModal with <iframe>).
            Now uses the same openPostPopup() as feed — REST API, no reload.
        -->
        <div class="grid-item"
             th:each="post : ${posts}"
             th:attr="data-post-id=${post.id}"
             onclick="openPostPopup(this.dataset.postId)">

            <img th:if="${not #lists.isEmpty(post.carouselMedia) and post.carouselMedia[0].mediaType == 'IMAGE'}"
                 th:src="${post.carouselMedia[0].mediaUrl}" th:alt="${post.caption}"/>

            <video th:if="${not #lists.isEmpty(post.carouselMedia) and post.carouselMedia[0].mediaType == 'VIDEO'}"
                   th:src="${post.carouselMedia[0].mediaUrl}" muted></video>

            <span th:if="${not #lists.isEmpty(post.carouselMedia) and post.carouselMedia[0].mediaType == 'VIDEO'}"
                  class="video-badge"><i class="fa-solid fa-play"></i></span>

            <span th:if="${#lists.size(post.carouselMedia) > 1}" class="carousel-badge">
                <i class="fa-solid fa-layer-group"></i>
            </span>

            <div class="grid-overlay">
                <span class="grid-stat">
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-heart"></i>
                    <span th:text="${post.likes != null ? post.likes.size() : 0}">0</span>
                </span>
                <span class="grid-stat">
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-comment"></i>
                    <span th:text="${post.comments != null ? post.comments.size() : 0}">0</span>
                </span>
            </div>

<!-- ── Post popup ── -->
<div id="ppOverlay" class="pp-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)closePP()">
    <div class="pp-card">
        <div class="pp-left" id="ppLeft">
            <button class="pp-nav pp-prev" onclick="ppNav(-1)">&#8249;</button>
            <div id="ppMedia" style="width:100%;height:100%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;"></div>
            <button class="pp-nav pp-next" onclick="ppNav(1)">&#8250;</button>
            <div class="pp-dots" id="ppDots"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="pp-right">
            <div class="pp-header">
                <div class="pp-av" id="ppAv"></div>
                <span class="pp-owner" id="ppOwner"></span>
                <button class="pp-close" onclick="closePP()"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark"></i></button>
            </div>
            <div class="pp-scroll" id="ppScroll">
                <div class="pp-spin-wrap"><div class="pp-spinner"></div></div>
            </div>
            <div class="pp-footer">
                <div class="pp-actions">
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" id="ppLikeBtn" onclick="ppLike()" title="Like">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-heart" id="ppLikeIcon"></i>
                    </button>
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" onclick="document.getElementById('ppInput').focus()" title="Comment">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-comment"></i>
                    </button>
                    <button class="pp-act-btn" title="Share">
                        <i class="fa-regular fa-paper-plane"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="pp-like-count" id="ppLikeCount"></div>
                <div class="pp-time" id="ppTime"></div>
                <div class="pp-reply-bar" id="ppReplyBar">
                    <span>Replying to <strong id="ppReplyLabel"></strong></span>
                    <button class="pp-cancel-reply" onclick="ppCancelReply()">&#10005;</button>
                </div>
                <div class="pp-input-row">
                    <input class="pp-input" id="ppInput" type="text"
                           placeholder="Add a comment…" autocomplete="off"
                           oninput="document.getElementById('ppPostBtn').disabled=!this.value.trim()"/>
                    <button class="pp-post-btn" id="ppPostBtn" disabled onclick="ppSubmit()">Post</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script th:inline="javascript">
    /* ── CSRF ── */
    const csrfToken  = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf"]').getAttribute('content');
    const csrfHeader = document.querySelector('meta[name="_csrf_header"]').getAttribute('content');
    const currentUserId = /*[[${currentUser.id}]]*/ null;

    function secureHeaders(json) {
        const h = { [csrfHeader]: csrfToken };
        if (json) h['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
        return h;
    }

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       BIO RENDERER
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    (function () {
        const bioEl = document.getElementById('bioText');
        if (!bioEl) return;
        const raw = bioEl.getAttribute('data-bio') || '';
        if (!raw.trim()) { bioEl.textContent = 'No bio yet.'; return; }
        const urlRe = /(https?:\/\/[^\s]+|www\.[^\s]+)/g;
        bioEl.innerHTML = '';
        raw.split(urlRe).forEach(part => {
            if (urlRe.test(part)) {
                const a = document.createElement('a');
                a.href = part.startsWith('http') ? part : 'https://' + part;
                a.textContent = part; a.target = '_blank'; a.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
                a.className = 'bio-link'; bioEl.appendChild(a);
            } else { bioEl.appendChild(document.createTextNode(part)); }
        });
    })();

    /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════
       POST POPUP  (identical logic as feed.html)
    ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
    let ppMediaList = [], ppMediaIdx = 0, ppPostId = null, ppReplyId = null;

    function openPostPopup(postId) {
        ppPostId = postId;
        ppMediaList = []; ppMediaIdx = 0; ppReplyId = null;
        document.getElementById('ppOverlay').classList.add('pp-open');
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        document.getElementById('ppScroll').innerHTML =
            '<div class="pp-spin-wrap"><div class="pp-spinner"></div></div>';

        fetch('/posts/' + postId + '/data')
            .then(r => { if (!r.ok) throw new Error(r.status); return r.json(); })
            .then(renderPopup)
            .catch(err => {
                document.getElementById('ppScroll').innerHTML =
                    '<p style="color:#e1306c;padding:20px;text-align:center;">Failed to load post.</p>';
                console.error(err);
            });
    }

    function closePP() {
        document.getElementById('ppOverlay').classList.remove('pp-open');
        document.body.style.overflow = '';
        ppPostId = null; ppReplyId = null;
        ppCancelReply();
    }

    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closePP(); });

    function renderPopup(d) {
        ppMediaList = d.media || []; ppMediaIdx = 0;
        renderMedia();
        const av = document.getElementById('ppAv');
        if (d.user.profilePicUrl) av.innerHTML = `<img src="${esc(d.user.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/>`;
        else av.textContent = (d.user.username||'?').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
        document.getElementById('ppOwner').textContent = d.user.username;
        renderLike(d.liked, d.likeCount);
        document.getElementById('ppTime').textContent = fmtDate(d.createdAt);
        renderComments(d);
    }

    function renderMedia() {
        const wrap = document.getElementById('ppMedia');
        const dots = document.getElementById('ppDots');
        const prev = document.querySelector('.pp-prev');
        const next = document.querySelector('.pp-next');
        const m = ppMediaList[ppMediaIdx];
        if (!m) { wrap.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#8e8e8e">No media</p>'; return; }
        wrap.innerHTML = m.mediaType === 'IMAGE'
            ? `<img src="${esc(m.mediaUrl)}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:contain;" alt=""/>`
            : `<video src="${esc(m.mediaUrl)}" controls style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:contain;"></video>`;
        dots.innerHTML = '';
        ppMediaList.forEach((_, i) => {
            const d = document.createElement('div');
            d.className = 'pp-dot' + (i === ppMediaIdx ? ' active' : '');
            d.onclick = () => { ppMediaIdx = i; renderMedia(); };
            dots.appendChild(d);
        });
        prev.style.display = ppMediaList.length > 1 && ppMediaIdx > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
        next.style.display = ppMediaList.length > 1 && ppMediaIdx < ppMediaList.length - 1 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }

    function ppNav(dir) {
        const ni = ppMediaIdx + dir;
        if (ni < 0 || ni >= ppMediaList.length) return;
        ppMediaIdx = ni; renderMedia();
    }

    function renderLike(liked, count) {
        const icon = document.getElementById('ppLikeIcon');
        icon.className = liked ? 'fa-solid fa-heart' : 'fa-regular fa-heart';
        icon.style.color = liked ? '#ff3040' : '';
        document.getElementById('ppLikeCount').textContent =
            count > 0 ? count + (count === 1 ? ' like' : ' likes') : '';
    }

    function ppLike() {
        if (!ppPostId) return;
        fetch('/posts/' + ppPostId + '/like', { method: 'POST', headers: secureHeaders(false) })
            .then(r => r.json()).then(d => renderLike(d.liked, d.likeCount)).catch(console.error);
    }

    function renderComments(d) {
        const scroll = document.getElementById('ppScroll');
        scroll.innerHTML = '';
        if (d.caption) {
            const cap = document.createElement('div');
            cap.className = 'pp-caption';
            cap.innerHTML = buildAvHtml(d.user) +
                `<div class="pp-caption-text"><strong>${esc(d.user.username)}</strong>${esc(d.caption)}</div>`;
            scroll.appendChild(cap);
        }
        if (!d.comments || !d.comments.length) {
            scroll.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend','<div class="pp-no-comments">No comments yet.</div>');
            return;
        }
        d.comments.forEach(c => scroll.appendChild(buildCEl(c)));
    }

    function buildAvHtml(u) {
        return u.profilePicUrl
            ? `<div class="pp-c-av"><img src="${esc(u.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/></div>`
            : `<div class="pp-c-av">${(u.username||'?').charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>`;
    }

    function buildCEl(c) {
        const isOwner = c.userId === currentUserId;
        const avHtml  = c.profilePicUrl
            ? `<div class="pp-c-av"><img src="${esc(c.profilePicUrl)}" alt=""/></div>`
            : `<div class="pp-c-av">${(c.username||'?').charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>`;
        const el = document.createElement('div');
        el.className = 'pp-c';
        el.dataset.commentId = c.id;
        el.dataset.userId    = c.userId;
        el.innerHTML = `
            ${avHtml}
            <div class="pp-c-body">
              <div class="pp-c-text"><strong>${esc(c.username)}</strong>${esc(c.content)}</div>
              <div class="pp-c-meta">
                <span>${fmtDate(c.createdAt)}</span>
                <button class="pp-reply-btn" data-id="${c.id}" data-un="${esc(c.username)}">Reply</button>
                <button class="pp-del-btn ${isOwner?'show':''}" data-id="${c.id}">Delete</button>
              </div>
              ${c.replyCount > 0
                ? `<button class="pp-vr-btn" data-id="${c.id}" data-cnt="${c.replyCount}">
                     View ${c.replyCount} ${c.replyCount===1?'reply':'replies'}
                   </button>` : ''}
            </div>`;
        el.querySelector('.pp-reply-btn').onclick = function(){ ppStartReply(this.dataset.id, this.dataset.un); };
        const db = el.querySelector('.pp-del-btn');
        if (db) db.onclick = function(){ ppDelete(this.dataset.id, el); };
        const vr = el.querySelector('.pp-vr-btn');
        if (vr) vr.onclick = function(){ ppToggleReplies(this, c.id); };
        return el;
    }

    function ppStartReply(id, username) {
        ppReplyId = id;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyLabel').textContent = '@' + username;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyBar').classList.add('on');
        const inp = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        inp.placeholder = 'Reply to @' + username + '…'; inp.focus();
    }

    function ppCancelReply() {
        ppReplyId = null;
        document.getElementById('ppReplyBar').classList.remove('on');
        const inp = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        if (inp) { inp.placeholder = 'Add a comment…'; inp.value = ''; }
        const btn = document.getElementById('ppPostBtn');
        if (btn) btn.disabled = true;
    }

    function ppSubmit() {
        const inp = document.getElementById('ppInput');
        const content = inp.value.trim();
        if (!content || !ppPostId) return;
        const body = {
            postId:   parseInt(ppPostId),
            content,
            parentId: ppReplyId ? parseInt(ppReplyId) : null,
            replyingToUsername: ppReplyId
                ? document.getElementById('ppReplyLabel').textContent.replace('@','')
                : null
        };
        fetch('/posts/comments/add', { method:'POST', headers: secureHeaders(true), body: JSON.stringify(body) })
            .then(r => r.json())
            .then(nc => {
                inp.value = ''; document.getElementById('ppPostBtn').disabled = true;
                const rid = ppReplyId; ppCancelReply();
                if (!nc) return;
                const scroll = document.getElementById('ppScroll');
                const noC = scroll.querySelector('.pp-no-comments'); if (noC) noC.remove();

                if (rid) {
                    let rDiv = document.getElementById('pp-r-' + rid);
                    if (!rDiv) {
                        rDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        rDiv.className = 'pp-replies';
                        rDiv.id = 'pp-r-' + rid;

                        const parentEl = document.querySelector(`[data-comment-id="${rid}"] .pp-c-body`);
                        if (parentEl) parentEl.appendChild(rDiv);
                    }

                    rDiv.style.display = 'block';
                    rDiv.appendChild(buildCEl(nc));
                }
                else {
                    scroll.appendChild(buildCEl(nc)); scroll.scrollTop = scroll.scrollHeight;
                }
            }).catch(console.error);
    }
    function flattenReplies(replies) {
    let result = [];

    function dfs(list) {
        list.forEach(r => {
            result.push(r);
            if (r.replies && r.replies.length) {
                dfs(r.replies);
            }
        });
    }

    dfs(replies);
    return result;
}
    function ppToggleReplies(btn, parentId) {
        const cont = document.getElementById('pp-r-'+parentId);
        if (!cont) return;
        if (cont.dataset.loaded === 'true') {
            const hidden = cont.style.display === 'none';
            cont.style.display = hidden ? 'block' : 'none';
            btn.innerHTML = hidden
                ? 'Hide replies'
                : 'View '+btn.dataset.cnt+' '+(btn.dataset.cnt==1?'reply':'replies');
            return;
        }
        btn.textContent = 'Loading…';
        fetch('/comments/replies/'+parentId).then(r=>r.json()).then(replies=>{
            cont.innerHTML = '';
            const flatReplies = flattenReplies(replies);
             flatReplies.forEach(r => cont.appendChild(buildCEl(r)));
            cont.dataset.loaded = 'true'; cont.style.display = 'block';
            btn.textContent = 'Hide replies';
        }).catch(()=>{ btn.textContent = 'View '+btn.dataset.cnt+' replies'; });
    }

    function ppDelete(id, el) {
        fetch('/comments/delete/'+id, { method:'POST', headers: secureHeaders(false) })
            .then(r => {
                if (r.ok) { el.remove(); const rd=document.getElementById('pp-r-'+id); if(rd)rd.remove(); }
                else alert('Could not delete comment.');
            }).catch(console.error);
    }

    function esc(s){ const d=document.createElement('div'); d.textContent=s||''; return d.innerHTML; }
    function fmtDate(iso){
        if(!iso)return'';
        try{ return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'}); }
        catch(e){return'';}
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

</head>
<body>
<div class="wrapper">
    <div class="card">
        <div class="logo">Instagram</div>
        <p class="tagline">Sign up to see photos and videos from your friends.</p>

        <div th:if="${error}" class="alert" th:text="${error}"></div>

        <form th:action="@{/users/register}" method="post" th:object="${user}">
            <div class="field">
                <input type="email" id="email" th:field="*{email}" placeholder="email" required/>
                <label for="email">Email</label>
            </div>
            <div class="field">
                <input type="text" id="username" th:field="*{username}" placeholder="username" required/>
                <label for="username">Username</label>
            </div>
            <div class="field">
                <input type="password" id="password" th:field="*{password}" placeholder="password" required/>
                <label for="password">Password</label>
            </div>
            <button type="submit" class="btn-signup">Sign up</button>
            <p class="terms">
                By signing up, you agree to our <a href="#">Terms</a>,
                <a href="#">Privacy Policy</a> and <a href="#">Cookies Policy</a>.
            </p>
        </form>
    </div>
    <div class="login-card">
        Have an account? <a th:href="@{/login}">Log in</a>
    </div>
</div>
